Subject: QTP update:



I saw tonight's results and was surprised to see # of failing scripts 
increased to 9(from 4), After couple of tries from Home realized that the 
server at times can be unresponsive because it also hosts PSTImport/MAPI and 
other tests but the other thing I noticed was that As soon as we log in, 
Zimbra becomes unresponsive for couple of seconds during which it loads 
OverviewPanel . If QTP tries to do any activity(like clicking on New btn or 
clicking on message), QTP clicks but nothing happens.

Just now checked in fixes that should fix both issues to a great extent, of 
course if the server becomes super-slow, then would break.


Details of the check in:
bug:none
Added logic to wait for overviewPanel - this would slow the login by couple 
of seconds and the suite by about 20 minutes in total, but would give much 
reliable results.
made logic changes to work for slower networks AND application 
not-responding as soon as we login.
loginFunctions:
As soon as we log in, Zimbra becomes unresponsive for couple of seconds 
during which it loads OverviewPanel. If QTP tries to do any activity(like 
clicking on New btn or clicking on message), QTP clicks but Zimbra wont 
respond.
Added logic to wait for overviewPanel - this would slow the login by couple 
of seconds and the suite by about 20 minutes in total, but would give much 
reliable results.

ButtonFunctions - Added some extra loopCycles to wait when trying to click 
on a btn but the btn is Disabled.
